### [328] [Scheduling with Time Dependent Utilities: Fairness and Efficiency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28800)
*Gaia Nicosia,Andrea Pacifici,Ulrich Pferschy*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 研究多智能体单机调度问题，目标是最大化所有智能体中的最小效用（公平性），分析不同变体的复杂度并提出求解方法，包括带释放/截止日期、线性效用函数调整、重调度和双层优化等场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多智能体调度中，每个作业对应一个自私的智能体，其效用随完成时间递减。传统调度目标可能不公平，因此需要研究公平导向的目标，即最大化所有智能体中的最小效用，确保没有智能体被严重忽视。

Method: 1) 提出二分搜索和精确贪婪算法求解一般情况；2) 分析带释放/截止日期的变体，证明复杂度（强NP难、弱NP难、多项式可解）；3) 研究线性效用函数在预算约束下的调整；4) 考察重调度问题，插入新作业并保持效用下界；5) 设计双层优化框架，领导者通过修改效用函数引导跟随者产生目标调度。

Result: 1) 一般情况可通过二分搜索和贪婪算法求解；2) 带释放日期的变体是强NP难的，但若只有一个作业有释放日期则是弱NP难的，当所有作业处理时间相同时是多项式可解的；3) 分析了效用函数调整对最优调度的影响；4) 提出了重调度问题的下界约束；5) 建立了双层优化模型，领导者可通过修改效用函数实现目标调度。

Conclusion: 该研究为多智能体调度引入了公平性目标（最大化最小效用），系统分析了不同变体的计算复杂度，提出了多种求解方法，并扩展到效用函数调整、重调度和双层优化等实际场景，为调度理论、多智能体系统和算法公平性领域做出了贡献。

Abstract: A new class of multi agent single machine scheduling problems is introduced, where each job is associated with a self interested agent with a utility function decreasing in completion time. We aim to achieve a fair solution by maximizing the minimum utility across all agents. We study the problem's complexity and propose solution methods for several variants. For the general case, we present a binary search procedure to find the largest possible minimum utility, as well as an exact greedy based alternative. Variants with release and due dates are analyzed, showing strong NP hardness for arbitrary release dates, but weak NP hardness for a single release date job, and polynomial solvability when all jobs share processing times. For all these cases we also study the corresponding problem of finding efficient solutions where the sum of utilities is maximized.
  We also examine settings where linear utility functions can be adjusted within budget constraints, exploring the impact on optimal schedules when intercepts or slopes are modified. From a single agent perspective, we investigate the effect of improving one agent's utility in the overall solution. Adding a new job to be inserted with the best possible utility gives rise to rescheduling problems, where different lower bounds depending on the utilities of the original fair schedule are imposed. Finally, we consider a bi level setting where a leader wants to enforce a certain target schedule by modifying utility functions while the follower computes a fair solution for the modified instance. Our work contributes to scheduling theory, multi agent systems, and algorithmic fairness, highlighting fairness oriented objectives in competitive scheduling.

</details>


### [329] [Incentives, Equilibria, and the Limits of Healthcare AI: A Game-Theoretic Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28825)
*Ari Ercole*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 该论文提出三种AI技术类型，并通过博弈论分析指出，仅优化任务而不改变激励机制无法改变医疗系统结果，只有重塑风险分配的干预措施才能改变系统行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI被广泛宣传为解决医疗容量和生产力压力的技术方案，但部署AI系统成本高昂，且其作为"万能解决方案"的乐观预期是否合理尚不明确。需要分析AI技术如何真正影响医疗系统结果。

Method: 提出三种AI技术原型：减少工作量的AI、增加可观测性的AI、机制层面激励改变的AI。使用简化的住院容量信号示例和最小博弈论推理进行分析。

Result: 分析表明，当激励机制保持不变时，仅进行任务优化不太可能改变系统结果。只有能够重塑风险分配的干预措施才能合理改变稳定的系统级行为。

Conclusion: 医疗领导层和采购决策应关注能够改变激励机制和风险分配的AI技术，而非仅仅优化任务的AI。这对医疗系统的AI部署策略有重要启示。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence (AI) is widely promoted as a promising technological response to healthcare capacity and productivity pressures. Deployment of AI systems carries significant costs including ongoing costs of monitoring and whether optimism of a deus ex machina solution is well-placed is unclear. This paper proposes three archetypal AI technology types: AI for effort reduction, AI to increase observability, and mechanism-level incentive change AI. Using a stylised inpatient capacity signalling example and minimal game-theoretic reasoning, it argues that task optimisation alone is unlikely to change system outcomes when incentives are unchanged. The analysis highlights why only interventions that reshape risk allocation can plausibly shift stable system-level behaviour, and outlines implications for healthcare leadership and procurement.

</details>


### [330] [An Economic Framework for Generative Engines: Advertising or Subscription?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29071)
*Luyang Zhang,Cathy Jiao,Beibei Li,Chenyan Xiong*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 生成式搜索引擎面临广告与订阅的权衡：应采用临界规则，仅当广告即时收益超过无广告响应的长期价值时才显示广告


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式引擎（如ChatGPT、Google AI Overviews）通过合成响应让用户绕过第三方网站，减少了网站广告收入，但自身也面临货币化问题：是在合成响应中插入广告还是保持无广告以推动订阅转化

Method: 引入动态框架研究该问题，捕捉查询级别设计选择如何随时间影响用户参与度、留存率和订阅转化

Result: 最优策略遵循临界规则：仅当广告即时收益超过提供无广告响应的长期价值时才向用户显示广告。该临界值在广告收入高或用户对广告不敏感时向含广告响应移动，在订阅转化相对更有价值时向无广告响应移动。存在竞争对手时，最优策略进一步向无广告响应移动

Conclusion: 研究结果揭示了现实生成式引擎提供商采用增强用户体验和长期可持续性设计的激励，广告密集型货币化在用户可自由切换到替代方案时变得不可持续

Abstract: Generative Engines (GEs) such as ChatGPT and Google's AI Overviews are rapidly reshaping search economics by delivering synthesized responses that allow users to bypass third-party websites, cutting those sites' advertising revenue. Yet this shift also leaves GEs facing their own monetization problem: whether to insert ads into synthesized responses or keep them ad-free to drive subscription conversions. In this paper, we introduce a dynamic framework to study this problem, which captures how query-level design choices shape user engagement, retention, and subscription conversion over time. Using this framework, we show that the optimal policy follows a cutoff rule: ads should only be shown to users only when the immediate ad payoff exceeds the long-term value of providing ad-free responses. This cutoff shifts toward with-ad responses when i) ad revenue is high or ii) users are less sensitive to ads, and toward ad-free responses when iii) subscription conversion becomes relatively more valuable. In addition, the presence of rival GEs shifts the optimal policy further toward ad-free responses, as ad-heavy monetization becomes less sustainable when users can freely switch to alternatives. Our findings reveal incentives for real-life generative engine providers to adopt designs that enhance user experience and long-term sustainability.

</details>


### [331] [Differentiable Normative Guidance for Nash Bargaining Solution Recovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29297)
*Moirangthem Tiken Singh,Surajit Borkotokey,Rajnish Kumar*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 提出一个基于图扩散的框架，用于生成满足个体理性并近似纳什议价解的谈判效用分配，无需帕累托前沿知识。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成模型常学习次优人类行为，产生远离帕累托效率的解；而经典方法需要完整的帕累托前沿知识，这在现实数据集中不可得。

Method: 提出引导图扩散框架：将谈判建模为有向图，用图注意力捕捉不对称代理属性；条件扩散模型将图映射到效用向量；在反向扩散最后步骤应用可微分复合引导损失，惩罚个体理性违反和纳什乘积差距。

Result: 在合成数据上达到99.45%的纳什效率（与oracle相差0.55个百分点），在CaSiNo和Deal or No Deal数据集上分别达到54.24%和88.67%，比无约束生成基线提升20-60个百分点，且实现100%个体理性合规。

Conclusion: 该框架能够在没有帕累托前沿知识的情况下，生成满足个体理性并近似纳什议价解的谈判效用分配，显著优于现有方法。

Abstract: Autonomous artificial intelligence agents in negotiation systems must generate equitable utility allocations satisfying individual rationality (IR), ensuring each agent receives at least its outside option, and the Nash Bargaining Solution (NBS), which maximizes joint surplus. Existing generative models often learn suboptimal human behaviors, producing solutions far from Pareto efficiency, while classical methods require full Pareto frontier knowledge, which is unavailable in real datasets. We propose a guided graph diffusion framework that generates individually rational utility vectors while approximating the NBS without frontier knowledge at inference time. Negotiations are modeled as directed graphs with graph attention capturing asymmetric agent attributes, and a conditional diffusion model maps these to utility vectors. A differentiable composite guidance loss, applied in the final reverse diffusion steps, penalizes IR violations and Nash product gaps. We prove that, under sufficient penalty weighting, solutions enter the IR region in finite time. Across datasets, the method achieves 100% IR compliance. Nash efficiency reaches 99.45% on synthetic data (within 0.55 percentage points of an oracle), and 54.24% (CaSiNo) and 88.67% (Deal or No Deal), improving 20-60 percentage points over unconstrained generative baselines.

</details>


### [332] [Hierarchical Battery-Aware Game Algorithm for ISL Power Allocation in LEO Mega-Constellations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29506)
*Kangkang Sun,Jianhua Li,Xiuzhen Chen,Minyi Guo*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: HBAG算法为LEO巨型星座提供分层电池感知博弈框架，解决太阳能间歇性下的星间链路功率分配问题，在有限和巨型星座规模下均能收敛到均衡点，显著提升能量可持续性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LEO星座功率分配方法存在局限性：静态功率上限忽略实时电池状态和完整功率预算，导致日食期能量危机；学习型方法能捕捉电池动态但缺乏均衡保证且无法扩展到大型星座。

Method: 提出分层电池感知博弈（HBAG）算法，统一博弈论框架，采用分布式更新规则，在有限星座规模下收敛到变分均衡，在巨型星座规模下收敛到平均场均衡，无需算法重新设计。

Result: 在Starlink Shell A（172颗卫星）实验中，HBAG实现100%能量可持续率（比SATFLOW提升87.4个百分点），消除日食期电池耗尽，保持流违规率低于10%行业容忍度，线性扩展到5000颗卫星且每时隙运行时间小于75毫秒。

Conclusion: HBAG为LEO巨型星座提供可扩展、保证均衡的功率分配解决方案，有效解决太阳能间歇性挑战，在能量可持续性、性能保持和扩展性方面显著优于现有方法。

Abstract: Sustaining high inter-satellite link (ISL) throughput under intermittent solar harvesting is a fundamental challenge for LEO mega-constellations. Existing frameworks impose static power ceilings that ignore real-time battery state and comprehensive onboard power budgets, causing eclipse-period energy crises. Learning-based approaches capture battery dynamics but lack equilibrium guarantees and do not scale beyond small constellations. We propose the Hierarchical Battery-Aware Game (HBAG) algorithm, a unified game-theoretic framework for ISL power allocation that operates identically across finite and megaconstellation regimes. For finite constellations, HBAG converges to a unique variational equilibrium; as constellation size grows, the same distributed update rule converges to the mean field equilibrium without algorithm redesign. Comprehensive experiments on Starlink Shell A (172 satellites) show that HBAG achieves 100% energy sustainability rate (87.4 percentage points improvement over SATFLOW), eliminates eclipse-period battery depletion, maintains flow violation ratio below the 10% industry tolerance, and scales linearly to 5,000 satellites with less than 75 ms per-slot runtime.

</details>


### [333] [Query-Based Committee Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29729)
*Itay Asher Zimet,Shiri Alouf-Heffetz,Nimrod Talmon*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统多赢家投票规则需要完整的选民偏好信息，这在大规模或注意力有限的实际场景中不切实际。本文旨在探索在有限预算的结构化查询下，如何准确近似获胜委员会。

Method: 提出了基于查询的多赢家选举框架，通过候选子集的细化查询来获取选民偏好；分析了多种成本函数来建模回答查询的认知努力；提出了评估查询策略的公理性质；通过实验评估了多种选举模型下的简单查询式委员会选择规则。

Result: 实验结果表明，基于递归分割候选集的策略在查询成本与委员会准确性之间达到最佳平衡。在多个统计模型中，这些策略比替代查询类型更高效地近似k-Borda选举结果。

Conclusion: 精心设计的查询策略可以显著减少所需的偏好信息量，同时仍能产生高质量的委员会结果，表明基于查询的偏好获取是扩展多赢家决策的有前景方法。

Abstract: Purpose: Multiwinner voting rules typically require full knowledge of voter preferences, which becomes impractical in large-scale or attention-limited settings. This paper investigates how accurately a winning committee can be approximated when voter preferences are elicited using a limited budget of structured queries. Methods: We introduce a query-based framework for multiwinner elections in which voter preferences are elicited through refinement queries over subsets of candidates under a limited budget. We analyse several cost functions that model the cognitive effort needed to answer such queries, propose axiomatic properties for evaluating them, and experimentally evaluate simple query-based committee selection rules across multiple election models. Results: Experimental results show that strategies based on recursively splitting candidate sets provide the best trade-off between elicitation cost and committee accuracy. Across several statistical models, these strategies approximate the outcome of k-Borda elections significantly more efficiently than alternative query types. Conclusion: The results demonstrate that well-designed query strategies can substantially reduce the amount of preference information required while still producing high-quality committee outcomes, suggesting that query-based elicitation is a promising approach for scalable multiwinner decision-making.

### [334] [Performative Scenario Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29982)
*Quanyan Zhu,Zhengye Han*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 提出了一种针对决策依赖机会约束问题的执行性场景优化框架，通过交替数据生成和优化来寻找自洽均衡解


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统随机优化假设数据生成过程独立于决策，但现实中决策会主动影响数据分布（如AI安全中的对抗性攻击），需要新的框架来处理这种反馈循环

Method: 定义执行性解为自洽均衡，使用Kakutani不动点定理证明存在性；提出无模型、基于场景的近似方法，交替进行数据生成和优化；采用对数样本大小调度的随机不动点迭代算法

Result: 在温和正则条件下，证明了随机不动点迭代算法几乎必然收敛到唯一的执行性解；通过LLM越狱防护的应用验证了框架有效性，展示了防护分类器与对抗提示分布的协同演化和稳定均衡收敛

Conclusion: 该框架为决策依赖随机优化问题提供了理论保证和计算可行的解决方案，特别适用于AI安全等存在决策-数据反馈循环的领域

Abstract: This paper introduces a performative scenario optimization framework for decision-dependent chance-constrained problems. Unlike classical stochastic optimization, we account for the feedback loop where decisions actively shape the underlying data-generating process. We define performative solutions as self-consistent equilibria and establish their existence using Kakutani's fixed-point theorem. To ensure computational tractability without requiring an explicit model of the environment, we propose a model-free, scenario-based approximation that alternates between data generation and optimization. Under mild regularity conditions, we prove that a stochastic fixed-point iteration, equipped with a logarithmic sample size schedule, converges almost surely to the unique performative solution. The effectiveness of the proposed framework is demonstrated through an emerging AI safety application: deploying performative guardrails against Large Language Model (LLM) jailbreaks. Numerical results confirm the co-evolution and convergence of the guardrail classifier and the induced adversarial prompt distribution to a stable equilibrium.

</details>
